# nī

_PWG article — 97 sub-card(s), 517 sense(s) · RU 410/517 · EN 447/517_

## nī

`n_i~~h0_00_pwg00`


**forms)** *nī*, *nayati* und *˚te*
[DHĀTUP. 22,5.](https://www.sanskrit-lexicon.uni-koeln.de/scans/csl-westergaard/disp/index.php?section=22) neben *nayeta* ep. auch *nayīta*
[MBH. 5,1263.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?5.1263) [1339.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?5.1339) neben *anayat* ved. auch *anayīt; anaiṣīt, aneṣṭa*, ved. *neṣat, neṣati, neṣi, naiṣṭa, neṣatha, neṣṭa* (med.), *neṣa* imper. aor.
[AV. 7,97,2.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av07.097.html#av07.097.02) [12,3,16.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av12.003.html#av12.003.16) *neṣatu*
[P. 3,1,34](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/1/34), Vārtt.
[P. 3,1,85](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/1/85), Schol.; ved. *anītām, nītām; nināya, ninyatus, ninyus* (
[P. 6,4,82](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/6/4/82)), *nīnima*
[TS. 3,2,8,3](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/taittiriyas/app1?3,2,8,3), wo aber das Metrum *ninīma* fordert; ved. *ninīyāt, ninīthas*; ep. *nayāmāsa; ninye; neṣyāmi*; ep. auch *nayiṣyāmi, ˚ṣye; netā*, ep. auch *nayitā; netum*, ep. (auch
[AIT. BR.]) auch *nayitum; nītvā, ˚nīya*; pass. *nīyate, nīta* .

- **RU:** *nī*, *nayati* и *˚te*
[DHĀTUP. 22,5.](https://www.sanskrit-lexicon.uni-koeln.de/scans/csl-westergaard/disp/index.php?section=22) наряду с *nayeta* эп. также *nayīta*
[MBH. 5,1263.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?5.1263) [1339.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?5.1339) наряду с *anayat* ved. также *anayīt; anaiṣīt, aneṣṭa*, ved. *neṣat, neṣati, neṣi, naiṣṭa, neṣatha, neṣṭa* (med.), *neṣa* imper. aor.
[AV. 7,97,2.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av07.097.html#av07.097.02) [12,3,16.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av12.003.html#av12.003.16) *neṣatu*
[P. 3,1,34](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/1/34), Vārtt.
[P. 3,1,85](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/1/85), Schol.; ved. *anītām, nītām; nināya, ninyatus, ninyus* (
[P. 6,4,82](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/6/4/82)), *nīnima*
[TS. 3,2,8,3](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/taittiriyas/app1?3,2,8,3), однако метр требует *ninīma*; ved. *ninīyāt, ninīthas*; эп. *nayāmāsa; ninye; neṣyāmi*; эп. также *nayiṣyāmi, ˚ṣye; netā*, эп. также *nayitā; netum*, эп. (также
[AIT. BR.]) также *nayitum; nītvā, ˚nīya*; pass. *nīyate, nīta* .
- **EN:** *nī*, *nayati* and *˚te*
[DHĀTUP. 22,5.](https://www.sanskrit-lexicon.uni-koeln.de/scans/csl-westergaard/disp/index.php?section=22) beside *nayeta* ep. also *nayīta*

[P. 6,4,82](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/6/4/82)), *nīnima*
[TS. 3,2,8,3](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/taittiriyas/app1?3,2,8,3), where however the metre requires *ninīma*; ved. *ninīyāt, ninīthas*; ep. *nayāmāsa; ninye; neṣyāmi*; ep. also *nayiṣyāmi, ˚ṣye; netā*, ep. also *nayitā; netum*, ep. (also

[MATSYOP. 14. 18. 20. 22. fgg.] *tarusthalaṃ (pipīlikāḥ) nayanti (aṇḍakāni) nimnāt*
[VARĀH. BṚH. S. 94,59.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/brihatsam/app1?94,59) *bhadra na sarvametadvittaṃ gṛhaṃ prati netuṃ yujyate*
[PAÑCAT. 96,4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app2?96,4) *kasyedamuśīrānulepanaṃ mṛṇālavanti ca nalinīpattrāṇi nīyante* for whom
[ŚĀK. 31,7.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shakuntala/app2?31,7) *kasyedaṃ nīyate toyam*
[VID. 289.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest1/app3?289)

**10_exclude)** — 10) wegführen so v. a. ausschliessen von: *somāt*
[AIT. BR. 2,19](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?2,19) ; vgl. desid. 4.

- **RU:** — 10) уводить, так v. a. исключать от чего-либо: *somāt*
[AIT. BR. 2,19](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?2,19) ; vgl. desid. 4.
- **EN:** 10) to lead away, and thus v. a. to exclude from: *somāt*
[AIT. BR. 2,19](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?2,19); vgl. desid. 4.
  <sub>attested</sub>

**11_give_guidance)** — 11) med. Anleitung geben: *(saṃmānane): śāstre nayate = śāstrasthaṃ siddhāntaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ prāpayati*
[P. 1,3,36](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/36), Sch.
Nach [VOP. 23,28](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mugdhabodha/app1?23,28) bedeutet *śāstre nayate* bewandert sein in; *saṃmānana* wird ebend. in der Bed. von verehren aufgefasst, da *viṣṇuṃ nayate* als Beispiel gegeben wird.

- **RU:** — 11) med. давать наставление: *(saṃmānane): śāstre nayate = śāstrasthaṃ siddhāntaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ prāpayati*
[P. 1,3,36](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/36), Sch.
По [VOP. 23,28](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mugdhabodha/app1?23,28) *śāstre nayate* означает быть сведущим в чём-либо; *saṃmānana* понимает ebend. в Bed. в значении почитать, поскольку *viṣṇuṃ nayate* приводится в качестве примера.
- **EN:** 11) med. to give instruction, guidance: *(saṃmānane): śāstre nayate = śāstrasthaṃ siddhāntaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ prāpayati*
[P. 1,3,36](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/36), Sch.
According to [VOP. 23,28](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mugdhabodha/app1?23,28) *śāstre nayate* means to be versed in; *saṃmānana* the form ebend. is understood in the Bed. to mean to revere, since *viṣṇuṃ nayate* is given as the example.
  <sub>lexicographic</sub>

**12_ascertain)** — 12) Etwas herausbringen, hinter Etwas kommen, feststellen: *sīmāṃ prati samutpanne vivāde grāmayordvayoḥ . jyaiṣṭhe māsi nayetsīmāṃ suprakāśeṣu setuṣu ..*
[M. 8,245.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,245) *etairliṅgairnayetsīmāṃ rājā*
[252.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,252) [256. fg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,256) [YĀJÑ. 2,151. fg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/yajnavalkya/app1?2,151) *yathā nayatyasṛkpātairmṛgasya mṛgayuḥ padam . nayettathānumānena dharmasya nṛpatiḥ padam ..*
[M. 8,44.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,44) Nach [P. 1,3,36](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/36) in der Bed. *jñāna* (vgl. u. 11) med.: *tattvaṃ nayate = niścinoti*
Schol. — In der Stelle: *na śaktastāni (asurāṇāṃ trīṇi purāṇi) maghavā netuṃ sarvāyudhairapi*
[MBH. 7,9557](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.9557) ist wohl *jetuṃ* st. *netuṃ* zu lesen.
— Vgl. *naya, nayana, nayitavya, nayiṣṭha, nāya, nāyaka, nāyin, nīti, netar, netavya, netra, neya* .
- **EN:** 12) to find out, discover, ascertain: *sīmāṃ prati samutpanne vivāde grāmayordvayoḥ . jyaiṣṭhe māsi nayetsīmāṃ suprakāśeṣu setuṣu ..*
[M. 8,245.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,245) *etairliṅgairnayetsīmāṃ rājā*
[252.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,252) [256. fg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,256) [YĀJÑ. 2,151. fg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/yajnavalkya/app1?2,151) *yathā nayatyasṛkpātairmṛgasya mṛgayuḥ padam . nayettathānumānena dharmasya nṛpatiḥ padam ..*
[M. 8,44.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,44) According to [P. 1,3,36](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/36) in the Bed. *jñāna* (vgl. u. 11) med.: *tattvaṃ nayate = niścinoti*
Schol. — In the passage: *na śaktastāni (asurāṇāṃ trīṇi purāṇi) maghavā netuṃ sarvāyudhairapi*
[MBH. 7,9557](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.9557) one should probably read *jetuṃ* st. *netuṃ*.
— Vgl. *naya, nayana, nayitavya, nayiṣṭha, nāya, nāyaka, nāyin, nīti, netar, netavya, netra, neya*.

**12)** — 12) Etwas herausbringen, hinter Etwas kommen, feststellen: *sīmāṃ prati samutpanne vivāde grāmayordvayoḥ . jyaiṣṭhe māsi nayetsīmāṃ suprakāśeṣu setuṣu ..*
[M. 8,245.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,245) *etairliṅgairnayetsīmāṃ rājā*
[252.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,252) [256. fg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,256) [YĀJÑ. 2,151. fg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/yajnavalkya/app1?2,151) *yathā nayatyasṛkpātairmṛgasya mṛgayuḥ padam . nayettathānumānena dharmasya nṛpatiḥ padam ..*
[M. 8,44.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,44) Nach [P. 1,3,36](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/36) in der Bed. *jñāna* (vgl. u. 11) med.: *tattvaṃ nayate = niścinoti*
Schol. — In der Stelle: *na śaktastāni (asurāṇāṃ trīṇi purāṇi) maghavā netuṃ sarvāyudhairapi*
[MBH. 7,9557](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.9557) ist wohl *jetuṃ* st. *netuṃ* zu lesen.

- **RU:** — 12) выяснять что-либо, доходить до чего-либо, устанавливать: *sīmāṃ prati samutpanne vivāde grāmayordvayoḥ . jyaiṣṭhe māsi nayetsīmāṃ suprakāśeṣu setuṣu ..*
[M. 8,245.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,245) *etairliṅgairnayetsīmāṃ rājā*
[252.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,252) [256. fg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,256) [YĀJÑ. 2,151. fg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/yajnavalkya/app1?2,151) *yathā nayatyasṛkpātairmṛgasya mṛgayuḥ padam . nayettathānumānena dharmasya nṛpatiḥ padam ..*
[M. 8,44.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,44) По [P. 1,3,36](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/36) в Bed. *jñāna* (vgl. u. 11) med.: *tattvaṃ nayate = niścinoti*
Schol. — В месте: *na śaktastāni (asurāṇāṃ trīṇi purāṇi) maghavā netuṃ sarvāyudhairapi*
[MBH. 7,9557](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.9557) следует, вероятно, читать *jetuṃ* st. *netuṃ*.
  <sub>attested</sub>

## paryanunī

`n_i~~h0_10_paryanu`


**1)** — *paryanu* Jmd viele freundliche Worte geben, sehr bitten: *sarvātmanā paryanunīyamāno yadā na saumitririyāya yogam*
[R. 6,112,110.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?6,112,110)

- **RU:** — *paryanu* щедро осыпать кого-л. добрыми словами, усиленно просить: *sarvātmanā paryanunīyamāno yadā na saumitririyāya yogam*
[R. 6,112,110.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?6,112,110)
- **EN:** — *paryanu* to give someone many kind words, to entreat urgently: *sarvātmanā paryanunīyamāno yadā na saumitririyāya yogam*
[R. 6,112,110.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?6,112,110)
  <sub>attested</sub>

## pratyanunī

`n_i~~h0_11_pratyanu`


**1)** — *pratyanu*
 1) Jmd zum Nachgeben bringen: *na cainamaśakadbhānurahaṃ vā snehakāraṇaiḥ . purā pratyanunetum*
[MBH. 12,150.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.150)

- **RU:** — *pratyanu*
 1) склонять кого-л. к уступке: *na cainamaśakadbhānurahaṃ vā snehakāraṇaiḥ . purā pratyanunetum*
[MBH. 12,150.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.150)
- **EN:** — *pratyanu*
 1) to bring someone to yield, to make someone give way: *na cainamaśakadbhānurahaṃ vā snehakāraṇaiḥ . purā pratyanunetum*
[MBH. 12,150.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.150)
  <sub>attested</sub>

**2)** — 2) sich gegen Jmd oder Etwas erklären, nicht einverstanden sein mit Jmd oder Etwas: *bhavatāhamannasyāśucibhāvamālakṣya pratyanunītaḥ* wurde ich von dir Lügen gestraft
[MBH. 1,787.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.787) *etatpratyanunaye* dagegen lege ich Verwahrung ein
[736.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.736)

- **RU:** — 2) высказываться против кого-л. или чего-л., не соглашаться с кем-л. или с чем-л.: *bhavatāhamannasyāśucibhāvamālakṣya pratyanunītaḥ* был уличён тобою во лжи
[MBH. 1,787.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.787) *etatpratyanunaye* против этого я заявляю протест
[736.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.736)
- **EN:** — 2) to declare oneself against someone or something, to disagree with someone or something: *bhavatāhamannasyāśucibhāvamālakṣya pratyanunītaḥ* I was proved a liar by you
[MBH. 1,787.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.787) *etatpratyanunaye* against this I enter a protest
[736.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.736)
  <sub>attested</sub>

- **EN:** — 3) to let pass (time): *te 'bhinīyaivāhaḥ paśumālabhanta . tenābhinīyaiva rātreḥ prācaran*
[TBR. 1,5,9,6.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/taittiriyabr/app1?1,5,9,6) Vgl. u. *ati* .
  <sub>attested</sub>

**4)** — 4) *abhinīta* abgerichtet: *abhinītāśca (gajāḥ) śikṣābhiḥ*

[MBH. 12,201.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.201) [768.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.768) *etāvadabhinītārthamuktvā*

- **RU:** — 4) *abhinīta* дрессированный, обученный: *abhinītāśca (gajāḥ) śikṣābhiḥ*

- **EN:** — 4) *abhinīta* trained: *abhinītāśca (gajāḥ) śikṣābhiḥ*
[MBH. 6,1765.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?6.1765) formed, intelligent, clever, of a person

— Vgl. *abhinaya, ˚netavya, ˚neya* .

## avānī

`n_i~~h0_25_av_a`


**1)** — *avā*, *avānītā*
[ŚĀK. CH. 125,5] wohl fehlerhaft für *apanītā*; die andere Recension
([83,9]) hat st. dessen *hṛtā* .

- **RU:** — *avā*, *avānītā*
[ŚĀK. CH. 125,5] — вероятно, ошибочное чтение вместо *apanītā*; другая рецензия
([83,9]) имеет st., вместо которого *hṛtā*.
- **EN:** — *avā*, *avānītā*
[ŚĀK. CH. 125,5] probably erroneously for *apanītā*; the other recension
([83,9]) has st. whose *hṛtā* .
  <sub>attested</sub>

**6)** — 6) feststellen, einsetzen, lehren; verfassen: *dyūte purāṇairvyavahāraḥ praṇītastatrātyayo nāsti na saṃprahāraḥ*

[AV. 8,8,10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av08.008.html#av08.008.10) In der Stelle *bhadra na sarvametadvittaṃ gṛhaṃ pratinetuṃ yujyate*
[PAÑCAT. 96,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app2?96,4) ist, wie schon
[BENFEY] gethan hat, *prati* von *netuṃ* zu trennen (in's Haus tragen).

- **RU:** — 2) подводить, доставлять: *tebhya enānprati nayāmi baddhvā*
[AV. 8,8,10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av08.008.html#av08.008.10) В месте *bhadra na sarvametadvittaṃ gṛhaṃ pratinetuṃ yujyate*
[PAÑCAT. 96,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app2?96,4) следует, как уже
[BENFEY] сделал, отделить *prati* от *netuṃ* (вносить в дом).
- **EN:** 2) to lead to, bring to: *tebhya enānprati nayāmi baddhvā*
[AV. 8,8,10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av08.008.html#av08.008.10) In the passage *bhadra na sarvametadvittaṃ gṛhaṃ pratinetuṃ yujyate*
[PAÑCAT. 96,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app2?96,4) it is, as [BENFEY] has already done, *prati* to be separated from *netuṃ* (to carry into the house).
  <sub>attested</sub>

**3)** — 3) beimengen: *sthālīpāke ghṛtapiṇḍānpratinīyāśnāti*
[KAUŚ. 52. 20. 35. 87.]

* haviḥ): nāsomayājī saṃnayet*
[TS. 2,5,5,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/taittiriyas/app1?2,5,5,1)
[ŚAT. BR. 1,6,4,10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?1,6,4,10) [11.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?1,6,4,11) [2,4,4,15.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?2,4,4,15)

## nī

`n_i~~h0_zz_pw00`


**1)** **1.** √*nī*, *nayati, ˚te*
— 1〉 leiten, führen, lenken. *agram* Etwas (Gen.) anführen. Auch vom Ross, das den Wagen führt.
- **EN:** **1.** √*nī*, *nayati, ˚te*
— 1〉 to lead, guide, direct. *agram* to adduce, cite something (Gen.). Also of the horse that draws the chariot.

**2)** — 2〉 abführen, wegführen, fortbringen, fortschaffen; hinführen, hinbringen, hinschaffen, — zu (Acc., Acc. mit *prati* [[PAÑCAT. 96,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app2?96,4)], Dat. oder Loc.).
- **EN:** — 2〉 to lead away, carry away, remove, convey away; to lead towards, bring to, convey to (Acc., Acc. with *prati* [[PAÑCAT. 96,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app2?96,4)], Dat. or Loc.).

**3)** — 3〉 Med. und seltener Act. mit sich führen, — nehmen, heimführen (ein Weib).
- **EN:** — 3〉 Med. and less frequently Act. to take with one, take home, lead home (a wife).

**4)** — 4〉 heran-, herbeiziehen [311,13](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?311).
- **EN:** — 4〉 to draw near, draw towards oneself [311,13](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?311).

**5)** — 5〉 Jmd oder Etwas (Acc.) in ein Verhältniss, eine Lage, eines Zustand (Acc. einmal auch Loc.) bringen, — versetzen [MBH. 5,36,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhbomb/app1?5,36,4). Mit *˚sāt* verwandeln in.
- **EN:** — 5〉 to bring or place someone or something (Acc.) into a relation, a situation, a state (Acc. once also Loc.) [MBH. 5,36,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhbomb/app1?5,36,4). With *˚sāt* to transform into.

**6)** — 6〉 *daṇḍam* den Stock führen, so v. a. Strafe verhängen.
- **EN:** — 6〉 *daṇḍam* to wield the rod, hence v. a. to inflict punishment.

**7)** — 7〉 hintragen, wegtragen, forttragen, hintragen zu (Acc., Loc. oder Acc. mit *prati*), Jmdm (Gen. oder *˚artham*) Etwas bringen.
- **EN:** — 7〉 to carry there, carry away, carry off, carry to (Acc., Loc. or Acc. with *prati*), to bring something to someone (Gen. or *˚artham*).

**8)** — 8〉 eine Linie u. s. w. führen, so v. a. ziehen.
- **EN:** — 8〉 to draw a line u. s. w., hence v. a. to draw.

**9)** — 9〉 Processe, eine heilige Handlung führen, leiten.
- **EN:** — 9〉 to conduct, perform a legal proceeding or a sacred rite.

**10)** — 10〉 hinbringen, zubringen, verbringen (die Zeit).
- **EN:** — 10〉 to pass, spend (time).

**11)** — 11〉 wegführen, so v. a. ausschliessen von (Abl.).
- **EN:** — 11〉 to lead away, hence v. a. to exclude from (Abl.).

**12)** — 12〉 Etwas herausbringen, hinter Etwas kommen, feststellen [MBH. 12,132,21](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhbomb/app1?12,132,21). Mit *anyathā* anders auslegen.
- **EN:** — 12〉 to bring something out, get to the bottom of something, ascertain [MBH. 12,132,21](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhbomb/app1?12,132,21). With *anyathā* to interpret differently.

**13)** — 13〉 *Med. eine Anleitung geben, einführen in (Loc.).
- **EN:** — 13〉 *Med. to give instruction, to initiate into (Loc.).

**14)** — 14〉 *netum* [MBH. 7,9557](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.9557) fehlerhaft für *bhettum*.
- **EN:** — 14〉 *netum* [MBH. 7,9557](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.9557) corrupt for *bhettum*.

**caus)** — Caus. *nāyayati* Jmd oder Etwas durch Jmd (Instr.) wegführen —, wegtragen lassen zu (Acc.).
- **EN:** — Caus. *nāyayati* to cause someone or something to be led away or carried away by someone (Instr.) to (Acc.).

**desid-1)** — Desid. *ninīṣati, ninīṣate*
— 1〉 wegführen —, hinführen wollen nach oder zu (Acc. oder Dat.).
- **EN:** — Desid. *ninīṣati, ninīṣate*
— 1〉 to wish to lead away or lead toward or to (Acc. or Dat.).

**desid-2)** — 2〉 mit sich nehmen wollen.
- **EN:** — 2〉 to wish to take along.

**desid-3)** — 3〉 in einen Zustand bringen wollen, mit doppeltem Acc.
- **EN:** — 3〉 to wish to bring into a state, with double Acc.

**desid-4)** — 4〉 hinbringen —, verbringen wollen (die Zeit) [NAIṢ. 9,66].
- **EN:** — 4〉 to wish to pass or spend (time) [NAIṢ. 9,66].

**desid-5)** — 5〉 ausschliessen wollen von (Abl.).
- **EN:** — 5〉 to wish to exclude from (Abl.).

**desid-6)** — 6〉 herauszubringen versuchen, nachspüren.
- **EN:** — 6〉 to try to ascertain, to investigate.

**intens)** — Intens. *nenīyate* gefangen führen, in seiner Gewalt haben. Scheinbar mit pass. Bed. [MBH. 12,7082](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.7082) (12,194,17) und [10502](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.10502) (12,285,18; es ist aber wie [12,8989](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.8989) (12,248,16) *guṇān* st. *guṇais* zu lesen.
- **EN:** — Intens. *nenīyate* to lead captive, to hold in one's power. Apparently with pass. Bed. [MBH. 12,7082](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.7082) (12,194,17) and [10502](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.10502) (12,285,18; but it is to be read like [12,8989](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.8989) (12,248,16) *guṇān* st. *guṇais*.

**pref-abhi)** — Mit *accha* Jmd hinführen —, leiten zu (Acc.).
- **EN:** — With *accha* to lead or guide someone to (Acc.).

**pref-ati-1)** — Mit *ati*
— 1〉 hinüberführen —, hinausführen —, hinüberhelfen über (Acc.).
- **EN:** — With *ati*
— 1〉 to lead across, lead out, help across (Acc.).

**pref-ati-2)** — 2〉 verstreichen lassen.
- **EN:** — 2〉 to let pass, allow to elapse.

**pref-adhi)** — Intens. vorwärts bringen.
- **EN:** — Intens. to bring forward, advance.

**pref-anu)** — Mit *abhyati* bringen auf (Loc.).
- **EN:** — With *abhyati* to bring onto (Loc.).

**pref-ava)** — Mit *vyati* verstreichen lassen.
- **EN:** — With *vyati* to let pass, allow to elapse.

**pref-apa-1)** — Mit *adhi*
— 1〉 abführen von (Abl.).
- **EN:** — With *adhi*
— 1〉 to lead away from (Abl.).

**pref-apa-2)** — 2〉 über das gewöhnliche Maass hinausführen, steigern.
- **EN:** — 2〉 to lead beyond the ordinary measure, to intensify, increase.

**pref-upa-1)** — Mit *anu*
— 1〉 geleiten, hingeleiten auf oder zu (Acc.).
- **EN:** — With *anu*
— 1〉 to escort, conduct to or onto (Acc.).

**pref-upa-2)** — 2〉 Jmdm (Dat.) Etwas (Acc.) zuführen, mittheilen.
- **EN:** — 2〉 to convey, communicate something (Acc.) to someone (Dat.).

**pref-upa-3)** — 3〉 (an sich heranziehen) Jmdm freundlich zu reden, freundliche Worte an Jmd richten in der Absicht ihn günstig zu stimmen, zu gewinnen, zu versöhnen, Jmd bitten; mit Acc. (einmal auch Gen. oder Dat.). *anunīta* gebeten, — um (Dat.).
- **EN:** — 3〉 (to draw towards oneself) to speak kindly to someone, to address friendly words to someone with the intention of winning his favour, gaining him over, reconciling him, to entreat someone; with Acc. (once also Gen. or Dat.). *anunīta* entreated, — for (Dat.).

**pref-upa-4)** — 4〉 *anunīta* ausgesöhnt.
- **EN:** — 4〉 *anunīta* reconciled.

**pref-upa-note)** — Desid. in *anuninīṣā* ([Nachtr. 2]).
- **EN:** — Desid. in *anuninīṣā* ([Nachtr. 2]).

**pref-sam-upa)** — Mit *paryanu* Jmd (Acc.) viele freundliche Worte geben, sehr bitten.
- **EN:** — With *paryanu* to give someone (Acc.) many friendly words, to entreat earnestly.

**pref-abhi-upa)** — Mit *pratyanu* Jmd in Bezug auf Etwas gute Worte geben; mit doppeltem Acc. [41,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?41). [43,17](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?43). Jmd zum Nachgeben bringen.
- **EN:** — With *pratyanu* to give someone kind words regarding something; with double Acc. [41,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?41). [43,17](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?43). To bring someone to yield, to persuade someone.

**pref-nis-1)** — Mit *apa*
— 1〉 wegführen, abführen, entfernen.
- **EN:** — With *apa*
— 1〉 to lead away, carry off, remove.

**pref-nis-2)** — 2〉 rauben stehlen, fortnehmen, wegschleppen.
- **EN:** — 2〉 to rob, steal, take away, drag off.

**pref-nis-3)** — 3〉 verscheuchen, entfernen, wegnehmen, wegschaffen. *hṛdayāt* sich Etwas aus dem Sinne schlagen.
- **EN:** — 3〉 to drive away, remove, take away, convey away. *hṛdayāt* to put something out of one's mind.

**pref-nis-4)** — 4〉 Fesseln, Kleider, Schmucksachen u. s. w. abnehmen, abziehen, ablegen [KĀD. 2,75,22].
- **EN:** — 4〉 to take off, remove, lay aside fetters, garments, ornaments u. s. w. [KĀD. 2,75,22].

**pref-nis-5)** — 5〉 weglassen, ausfallen lassen (eine Silbe) [VAITĀN.]
- **EN:** — 5〉 to omit, drop (a syllable) [VAITĀN.]

**pref-nis-6)** — 6〉 ausziehen, gewinnen aus (Abl.).
- **EN:** — 6〉 to extract, derive from (Abl.).

**pref-nis-7)** — 7〉 ausnehmen, ausschliessen (aus einer Regel).
- **EN:** — 7〉 to except, exclude (from a rule).

**pref-nis-8)** — 8〉 erkennen [BHĀG. P. 5,18,33](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?5,18,33).
- **EN:** — 8〉 to recognize, discern [BHĀG. P. 5,18,33](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?5,18,33).

**pref-nis-9)** — 9〉 *apanīta* ausser weggeführt u. s. w. auch abgeführt von, so v. a. im Widerspruch stehend mit (mit Comp. vorangehend) und zu Leide gethan ([LALIT. 162,15]). Vgl. auch *apnīta*.
- **EN:** — 9〉 *apanīta* besides 'led away' u. s. w. also 'led off from', hence v. a. 'in contradiction with' (preceded by Comp.) and 'done harm to' ([LALIT. 162,15]). Vgl. also *apnīta*.

**pref-nis-desid)** — Desid. zu entfernen wünschen.
- **EN:** — Desid. to wish to remove.
